<title>All Dead, All Dead - World&#39;s Largest List of Deceased Musicians [Page 12] - Rate Your Music</title>
      <meta name="description" content="These are the dead [b][i]in my collection[/i][/b]. Musicians who (already) left the stage of life. This is a list to honor their work - to remember - and to discover the great heavenly jukebox.

You&#39;ll see the musical skills they are most famous for. That means I will list one or more instruments they played mainly. Regularly I won&#39;t list them as producer and composer, because most of them did both. Only when he or she was mainly noticed for producing or any other musical work (besides playing an instrument or singing) I will mention.

Many of those artists are known for their own work, their own records, their own songs. If possible I will give examples for that.
In many cases the played with other musicians; in bands or just on records in studio. I will try to give an example of that too.


This list is sorted by date of death.


Unfortunately - but naturally - a work in progress:

[b]Latest additions:[/b] [i]Bob Fish, Ralph Viera Tavares, Dick Halligan, Dean Daughtry, Willy Finlayson, Pooch Tavares, Dickey Betts, Henry Heinrich, Duane Eddy, Richard Tandy, David Sanborn [all: 2020s][/i] [Page 12]" />

                <meta property="og:title" content="All Dead, All Dead - World&#39;s Largest List of Deceased Musicians - RYM/Sonemic" /><meta property="og:description" content="These are the dead [b][i]in my collection[/i][/b]. Musicians who (already) left the stage of life. This is a list to honor their work - to remember - and to discover the great heavenly jukebox.

You&#39;ll see the musical skills they are most famous for. That means I will list one or more instruments they played mainly. Regularly I won&#39;t list them as producer and composer, because most of them did both. Only when he or she was mainly noticed for producing or any other musical work (besides playing an instrument or singing) I will mention.

Many of those artists are known for their own work, their own records, their own songs. If possible I will give examples for that.
In many cases the played with other musicians; in bands or just on records in studio. I will try to give an example of that too.


This list is sorted by date of death.


Unfortunately - but naturally - a work in progress:

[b]Latest additions:[/b] [i]Bob Fish, Ralph Viera Tavares, Dick Halligan, Dean Daughtry, Willy Finlayson, Pooch Tavares, Dickey Betts, Henry Heinrich, Duane Eddy, Richard Tandy, David Sanborn [all: 2020s][/i] [Page 12]" />

                       }
                     });

                }

   function doFlag ( assoc_id, type, flag, polarity ) {

      hideflag();
      did('flagimg_' + assoc_id + '_' + type).src = '//e.snmc.io/2.5/img/images/loading.gif';
      sendRequest('FlagItem|' + token + '|' + assoc_id + '|' + type + '|' + flag + '|' + polarity);
   }


   var flagAssocId = 0;
   var flagType = 's';
   var currentFlag = '';

   function flagItem(assoc_id, type, event) { 
      if ( did('flag_' + assoc_id + '_' + type).className != 'flag0' )
      {
          doFlag ( assoc_id, flagType, '', 0 );
          return;
      }

     var fl = document.getElementById('flag');
   
     var pageX, pageY;
   
     if (event.pageX) {
         pageX = event.pageX;
     } else { 
         pageX = event.clientX + document.documentElement.scrollLeft;
     }
     if (event.pageY )
     {
         pageY = event.pageY;
     } else {  
         pageY = event.clientY +  document.documentElement.scrollTop;
     }
   
     fl.style.top = pageY + 'px';
     fl.style.left = pageX+ 'px';
     fl.style.visibility='visible';
     flagAssocId = assoc_id;
   
   }

   function hideflag() {
    document.getElementById('flag').style.visibility='hidden';
   }

<div class="large-8 columns" style="padding:1.5em;">
<h1 style="font-size:2.1em">All Dead, All Dead - World&#39;s Largest List of Deceased Musicians</h1>

<p style="font-size:1.6em">A list by <a class="user" href = "/~montezuma <view-source:https://rateyourmusic.com/~montezuma>">montezuma</a></p><p>Categories: <span class="rendered_text"><a title="[Descriptor21997]" class="genre" href="/list_classifier/Artist/ <view-source:https://rateyourmusic.com/list_classifier/Artist/>">Artist</a></span></p>
<p style="color:var(--mono-6)">[List366832] |  <a class="fav0" title="add/remove favorite" id="link_366832_s_f" href="javascript:void(0);" onClick="javascript:toggleFav('366832', 's', 'f');" ><img id="fav_366832_s_f" alt="heart" src="//e.snmc.io/2.5/img/images/hearte.gif <view-source:https://e.snmc.io/2.5/img/images/hearte.gif>" width="18" height="18" /></a><a class="fav1 subtext" href="/favorited/366832_s_f <view-source:https://rateyourmusic.com/favorited/366832_s_f>"><span id="favtext_366832_s_f" class="smallgray">+118</span></a> </p>
  <div style="float:left;padding-right:15px;padding-bottom:15px;"><img id="img_s_366832"   src="//e.snmc.io/i/300/w/794500ca9e0a52b67017b5be32236448/12118944 <view-source:https://e.snmc.io/i/300/w/794500ca9e0a52b67017b5be32236448/12118944>" width="300" height="168" alt="David Sanborn" title="David Sanborn" border="0" /><br><span style="font-size:9px">David Sanborn</span></div>
  <span class="rendered_text">These are the dead <b><i>in my collection</i></b>. Musicians who (already) left the stage of life. This is a list to honor their work - to remember - and to discover the great heavenly jukebox.<br /><br />You&#39;ll see the musical skills they are most famous for. That means I will list one or more instruments they played mainly. Regularly I won&#39;t list them as producer and composer, because most of them did both. Only when he or she was mainly noticed for producing or any other musical work (besides playing an instrument or singing) I will mention.<br /><br />Many of those artists are known for their own work, their own records, their own songs. If possible I will give examples for that.<br />In many cases the played with other musicians; in bands or just on records in studio. I will try to give an example of that too.<br /><br /><br />This list is sorted by date of death.<br /><br /><br />Unfortunately - but naturally - a work in progress:<br /><br /><b>Latest additions:</b> <i>Bob Fish, Ralph Viera Tavares, Dick Halligan, Dean Daughtry, Willy Finlayson, Pooch Tavares, Dickey Betts, Henry Heinrich, Duane Eddy, Richard Tandy, David Sanborn [all: 2020s]</i></span>



</div> <div class="large-4 columns" style="min-width:400px;min-height:300px;">
